# Business Universe Coverage Report

This is an internal evidence source. It does not authorize implementation, completion, release, or production.

## Human Summary

我已把当前任务拆成六类独立行为，并补齐参与者、来源、选择、传播、一致性、失败、恢复和审计路径。独立 Challenger 已逐场景复核通过；实现、验证和最终完成仍由后续统一链路判断。

## Categories, Participants, Origins, And Paths

- `category:consumer-chain`: Same-task required-consumer and evidence-authority chain (`EVIDENCE_BOUND`)
- `category:controlled-apply`: Atomic controlled apply, receipt, rollback, and recovery (`EVIDENCE_BOUND`)
- `category:existing-adoption`: Request-bound existing-project adoption and future-session activation (`EVIDENCE_BOUND`)
- `category:baseline-integrity`: Goal-derived platform baseline, pack installation, and industrial evidence integrity (`EVIDENCE_BOUND`)
- `category:source-release-trust`: Source release candidate trust and exact external-effect boundary (`EVIDENCE_BOUND`)
- `category:distributed-consumer-activation`: Source-to-generated-to-installed consumer activation and parity (`EVIDENCE_BOUND`)

Participants are explicit: Codex, current project authority, the solo user's real-world consent role, external release provider, source distribution, and installed/fresh-session consumers.
